Jin sawaalon ko hum discuss karna chahte the unme se do abhi bhi discussion ke liye rehte hain; (3) kya ye wo aadmi hai jisne doosre ko usse zyada assign kiya hai jo unjustly act karta hai, ya wo jiske paas excessive share hai, aur (4) kya khud ko unjustly treat karna possible hai. Ye sawaal connected hain; kyunki agar pehla alternative possible hai aur distributor unjustly act karta hai aur wo aadmi nahi jiske paas excessive share hai, to agar ek aadmi doosre ko khud se zyada assign karta hai, knowingly aur voluntarily, wo khud ko unjustly treat karta hai; jo modest log karte lagte hain, kyunki virtuous aadmi apni share se kam lene ki tendency rakhta hai. Ya kya ye statement bhi qualification chahti hai? Kyunki (a) wo shayad kisi doosre good ka usse zyada share paata hai, jaise reputation ka ya intrinsic nobility ka. (b) Sawaal solve ho jaata hai wahi distinction apply karke jo humne unjust action par apply ki thi; kyunki wo apni khud ki wish ke contrary kuch bhi suffer nahi karta, isliye wo is extent tak unjustly treat nahi kiya jaata, balki zyada se zyada harm hi suffer karta hai.

Ye bhi plain hai ki distributor unjustly act karta hai, lekin hamesha wo aadmi nahi jiske paas excessive share hai; kyunki wo aadmi unjustly act nahi karta jise injustice ki jaati hai, balki wo jiske paas voluntarily unjust act karne ka right hai, yani wo person jisme action ka origin hai, aur ye distributor mein hai, receiver mein nahi. Phir, kyunki word 'do' ambiguous hai, aur ek sense hai jisme lifeless things, ya ek hand, ya ek servant jo order obey karta hai, slay karne wala kaha ja sakta hai, jo excessive share paata hai wo unjustly act nahi karta, halaanki wo unjust 'karta' hai.

Phir, agar distributor ne apna judgement ignorance mein diya, wo legal justice ke respect mein unjustly act nahi karta, aur uska judgement is sense mein unjust nahi hai, lekin ek sense mein ye unjust hai (kyunki law se just kya hai, aur primary way mein, different hain); lekin agar knowledge ke saath usne unjustly judge kiya, to wo khud gratitude ka ya revenge ka ek excessive share aim kar raha hai. Utna hi, to, jaise wo plunder mein share karega, jis aadmi ne in reasons ke liye unjustly judge kiya hai usne too much paaya hai; ki jo wo paata hai wo different hai jo wo distribute karta hai isse koi farak nahi padta, kyunki agar wo plunder mein share karne ke view se land award karta hai to wo land nahi money paata hai.

Men sochte hain ki unjustly act karna unki power mein hai, aur isliye ki just hona easy hai. Lekin ye nahi hai; apne neighbour ki wife ke saath lie karna, doosre ko wound karna, ek bribe deliver karna, easy hai aur hamari power mein hai, lekin in cheezon ko ek certain state of character ke result mein karna na easy hai na hamari power mein. Similarly just aur unjust ko jaanna, men sochte hain, koi great wisdom require nahi karta, kyunki laws dwara deal ki gayi matters ko samajhna hard nahi hai (halaanki ye wo cheezein nahi hain jo just hain, siwaye incidentally); lekin actions kaise done ki jaayein aur distributions effect ki jaayein taaki just hon, ise jaanna health ke liye kya good hai ise jaanne se ek greater achievement hai; halaanki wahan bhi, honey, wine, hellebore, cautery, aur knife ka use aise hain ye jaanna easy hai, lekin kaise, kis se, aur kab ye apply kiye jaane chahiye health produce karne ke view se, ye jaanna ek physician hone se kam achievement nahi hai. Phir, isi very reason ke liye men sochte hain ki unjustly act karna just aadmi ka characteristic hai unjust se kam nahi, kyunki wo in mein se har unjust acts karne mein less nahi balki even more capable hoga; kyunki wo ek woman ke saath lie kar sakta hai ya ek neighbour ko wound kar sakta hai; aur brave aadmi apna shield fenk sakta hai aur is direction ya us direction mein flight tak turn kar sakta hai. Lekin coward khelna ya unjustly act karna in cheezon ko karne mein consist nahi karta, siwaye incidentally, balki inhe ek certain state of character ke result mein karne mein, jaise medicine aur healing practise karna knife apply karne ya na karne mein consist nahi karta, medicines use karne ya na karne mein, balki ise ek certain way mein karne mein.

Just acts un logo ke beech occur karte hain jo khud mein good cheezon mein participate karte hain aur inme too much ya too little ho sakta hai; kyunki kuch beings (jaise presumably gods) inme too much nahi rakh sakte, aur doosron ke liye, jo incurably bad hain, inme se sabse smallest share bhi beneficial nahi hai balki sab aise goods harmful hain, jabki doosron ke liye wo ek point tak beneficial hain; isliye justice essentially kuch human hai.

**Equity, legal justice ka ek corrective**

**10.** Hamara agla subject equity aur equitable hai, aur unka justice aur just se respective relations. Kyunki examination par wo na to absolutely same lagte hain na hi generically different; aur jabki hum kabhi equitable aur equitable aadmi ki praise karte hain (isliye hum naam ko praise ke way mein doosri virtues ke instances tak bhi apply karte hain, 'good' ki jagah, 'more equitable' se matlab lete hue ki ek cheez better hai), doosre times, jab hum reason karte hain, ye strange lagta hai agar equitable, just se ek different cheez hote hue, phir bhi praiseworthy hai; kyunki ya to just ya equitable good nahi hai, agar wo different hain; ya, agar dono good hain, wo same hain.

Ye, to, kaafi hain wo considerations jo equitable ke baare mein problem ko rise dete hain; wo sab ek sense mein correct hain aur ek doosre ke opposed nahi hain; kyunki equitable, halaanki ye ek kism ki justice se better hai, phir bhi just hai, aur ye ek different class of thing hone ke roop mein nahi hai ki ye just se better hai. Wahi cheez, to, just aur equitable hai, aur jabki dono good hain equitable superior hai.

Jo problem create karta hai wo ye hai ki equitable just hai, lekin legally just nahi balki legal justice ka ek correction. Reason ye hai ki saara law universal hai lekin kuch cheezon ke baare mein ek universal statement banaana possible nahi hai jo correct ho. Un cases mein, to, jisme universally speak karna necessary hai, lekin correctly aisa karna possible nahi hai, law usual case leti hai, halaanki ye error ki possibility se ignorant nahi hai. Aur ye none the less correct hai; kyunki error na to law mein hai na legislator mein, balki cheez ki nature mein, kyunki practical affairs ka matter shuru se hi is kism ka hai. Jab law universally baat karti hai, to, aur usme ek case arise hota hai jo universal statement se covered nahi hai, tab ye right hai, jahan legislator humein fail karta hai aur over-simplicity se err kiya hai, omission ko correct karna — wo kehna jo legislator khud kehta agar wo present hota, aur apne law mein daalta agar use pata hota. Isi wajah se equitable just hai, aur ek kism ki justice se better — absolute justice se better nahi, balki us error se better jo statement ki absoluteness se arise hoti hai. Aur yahi equitable ki nature hai, law ka ek correction jahan ye apni universality ki wajah se defective hai. Fact mein yahi reason hai ki sab cheezein law se determine nahi ki jaati hain, namely, ki kuch cheezon ke baare mein law lay down karna impossible hai, isliye ek decree ki zaroorat hai. Kyunki jab cheez indefinite hai rule bhi indefinite hai, jaise leaden rule jo Lesbian moulding banaane mein use hota hai; rule khud ko stone ki shape ke adapt karta hai aur rigid nahi hai, aur isi tarah decree bhi facts ke adapted hai.

Ye plain hai, to, ki equitable kya hai, aur ki ye just hai aur ek kism ki justice se better hai. Isse ye bhi evident hai ki equitable aadmi kaun hai; wo aadmi jo aise acts choose aur karta hai, aur bad sense mein apne rights ke liye stickler nahi hai balki apni share se kam lene ki tendency rakhta hai halaanki uske paas law hai apne side par, equitable hai, aur ye state of character equity hai, jo ek kism ki justice hai aur ek different state of character nahi.

**Kya koi insaan khud ke saath unjustly treat kar sakta hai?**

**11.** Kya ek aadmi khud ko unjustly treat kar sakta hai ya nahi, ye jo kaha gaya hai usse evident hai. Kyunki (a) just acts ki ek class wo hai jo kisi bhi virtue ke saath accord karti hai aur law dwara prescribed hai; jaise law expressly suicide permit nahi karti, aur jo ye expressly permit nahi karti wo forbid karti hai. Phir, jab ek aadmi law ke violation mein doosre ko harm karta hai (retaliation mein alawa) voluntarily, wo unjustly act karta hai, aur ek voluntary agent wo hai jo dono person ko jaanta hai jise wo apni action se affect kar raha hai aur instrument jo wo use kar raha hai; aur jo anger se voluntarily khud ko stab karta hai wo ye life ke right rule ke contrary karta hai, aur ye law nahi allow karti; isliye wo unjustly act kar raha hai. Lekin kiske prati? Surely state ke prati, khud ke prati nahi. Kyunki wo voluntarily suffer karta hai, lekin koi bhi voluntarily unjustly treat nahi kiya jaata. Yahi bhi reason hai ki state punish karta hai; civil rights ka ek certain loss us aadmi ko attach hota hai jo khud ko destroy karta hai, is ground par ki wo state ko unjustly treat kar raha hai.

Further, (b) 'acting unjustly' ke us sense mein jisme jo aadmi 'unjustly act' karta hai wo sirf unjust hai aur poori tarah bad nahi, khud ko unjustly treat karna possible nahi hai (ye pehle sense se different hai; term ka unjust aadmi ek sense mein ek particularized way mein wicked hai jaise coward hai, wo poori tarah wicked hone ke sense mein nahi, isliye uska 'unjust act' general mein wickedness manifest nahi karta). Kyunki (i) isse ye imply hota ki same cheez ek hi same time par same cheez se subtract aur add ki gayi hai; lekin ye impossible hai — just aur unjust hamesha ek se zyada person involve karte hain. Further, (ii) unjust action voluntary hai aur choice se ki jaati hai, aur initiative leti hai (kyunki jo aadmi suffer karne ki wajah se return mein wahi karta hai use unjustly act karta nahi maana jaata); lekin agar ek aadmi khud ko harm karta hai wo same time par same cheezein suffer aur karta hai. Further, (iii) agar ek aadmi khud ko unjustly treat kar sakta, wo voluntarily unjustly treat kiya ja sakta. Besides, (iv) koi bhi bina particular injustice ke acts commit kiye unjustly act nahi karta; lekin koi bhi apni khud ki wife ke saath adultery ya apne khud ke house par housebreaking ya apni khud ki property par theft commit nahi kar sakta.

General mein, sawaal 'Kya ek aadmi khud ko unjustly treat kar sakta hai?' solve bhi hota hai wahi distinction se jo humne sawaal 'Kya ek aadmi voluntarily unjustly treat kiya ja sakta hai?' par apply kiya.

(Ye bhi evident hai ki dono bad hain, unjustly treat kiya jaana aur unjustly act karna; kyunki ek ka matlab hai less rakhna aur doosre ka more rakhna intermediate amount se, jo yahan wahi part play karta hai jo medical art mein healthy karta hai, aur bodily training ki art mein good condition karti hai. Lekin phir bhi unjustly act karna worse hai, kyunki isme vice involve hai aur ye blameworthy hai — vice involve karta hai jo ya to complete aur unqualified kism ka hai ya almost aisa hai (humein doosra alternative admit karna chahiye, kyunki sab voluntary unjust action state of character ke roop mein injustice imply nahi karta), jabki unjustly treat kiya jaana khud mein vice aur injustice involve nahi karta. Khud mein, to, unjustly treat kiya jaana kam bad hai, lekin isse rokne ke liye kuch nahi hai ki ye incidentally ek greater evil ho. Lekin theory isse koi parwaah nahi karti; ye pleurisy ko ek stumble se zyada serious mischief kehta hai; phir bhi doosra incidentally zyada serious ban sakta hai, agar isse hone wala fall aapko enemy dwara prisoner banaya jaana ya death diya jaana leads karta hai.)

Metaphorically aur ek certain resemblance ki wajah se ek justice hai, na ki ek aadmi aur khud ke beech, balki uske certain parts ke beech; phir bhi justice ki har kism nahi balki wo jo master aur servant ki hai ya husband aur wife ki. Kyunki ye wo ratios hain jinme soul ka wo part jiske paas rational principle hai wo irrational part se stand karta hai; aur inhi parts ke view se log ye bhi sochte hain ki ek aadmi khud ke prati unjust ho sakta hai, namely, kyunki ye parts apni respective desires ke contrary kuch suffer karne ke liable hain; isliye inke beech ek mutual justice maani jaati hai jaise ruler aur ruled ke beech.

Ise humara justice aur baaki, yani baaki moral, virtues ka account maan lete hain.
